##ICON ASSIGNMENT TARGETS

#level 1 strike
defined_text = {
	name = strike_level_tier1_icon
	#not selected
	text = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { strike_level_tier1_selected = 0 } }
		localization_key = GFX_WMD_strike_1_off
	}
	#selected
	text = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { strike_level_tier1_selected = 1 } }
		localization_key = GFX_WMD_strike_1_on
	}
}

		localization_key = "Level 3"	
	}
}

###################################
#STATUS BUTTONS
defined_text = {
	name = target_status
	#not selected
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { wmd_target_selected = 0 }
				check_variable = { wmd_num_targets_selected = 0 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_wmd_status_target_no
	}
	#selected
	text = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { wmd_target_selected = 1 }
			check_variable = { wmd_num_targets_selected > 0 }
		}
		localization_key = GFX_wmd_status_target_yes
	}
}

defined_text = { 
	name = missile_status
	#not selected
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { missile_selected = 0 }
				check_variable = { ROOT.wmd_num_targets_selected = 0 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_wmd_status_missile
	}
	#selected
	text = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { missile_selected = 1 }
				check_variable = { ROOT.wmd_num_targets_selected > 0 }
			}
		}
		localization_key = GFX_wmd_status_missile_yes
	}
}

# Confirm status
defined_text = {  
	name = confirm_status
	#not selected
	text = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { wmd_ready_status < 1 } }
		localization_key = GFX_wmd_ready_status_no
	}
	#selected
	text = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { wmd_ready_status = 1 } }
		localization_key = GFX_wmd_ready_status_yes
	}
}
